***паясничавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:паясничать.html>пая́сничавший</a> (27790)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:паясничать.html>пая́сничавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pajásničavšij</span>)

***певица.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:певица.html>певи́ца</a> (8694)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:певица.html>певи́ца</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pevíca</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:певица.html>певи́цы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:певица.html>певи́цы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:певица.html>певи́ц</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:певец.html>певе́ц</a></b>)

***пегий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пегий.html>пе́гий</a> (14213)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пѣгъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pěgŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:пегий.html>пе́га</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pega</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">freckle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">pingō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I paint</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пегий.html>пе́гий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pégij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)

***пекло.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пекло.html>пекло</a> (10900)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">пькъло</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pĭkŭlo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пекло.html>пе́кло</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">péklo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пекло.html>пе́кла</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>scorching heat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>Ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пекло.html>пе́кло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лице</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nu i <b>péklo</b> na úlice!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What a scorcher outside!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> heat (the height or stress of an action or condition)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пекло.html>пе́кло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сражение.html>сраже́ния</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:битва.html>би́твы</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бо́я</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>péklo</b> sražénija, bítvy, bója</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the heat of the battle</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>hell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> чёрта <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пекло.html>пе́кле</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u čórta v <b>pékle</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">with the devil in hell</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***пеленка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пеленка.html>пелёнка</a> (13704)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пеленка.html>пелёнка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peljónka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пеленка.html>пелёнки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пеленка.html>пелёнки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пеленка.html>пелёнок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nappy/diaper, swaddling cloth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пеленка.html>пелёнок</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>peljónok</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from the cradle</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выйти.html>вы́йти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пеленка.html>пелёнок</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">výjti iz <b>peljónok</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">be no longer a kid</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***пена.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пена.html>пе́на</a> (4669)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*pěna</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пена.html>пе́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">péna</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пена.html>пе́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пена.html>пе́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пена.html>пе́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> foam, spume, scum, froth</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lather</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пена.html>пе́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">péna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
